BYUNG NAS MTSAN DAD PA RGYAL POR BTAGS, KHA CHE PAn CHEN ZLA BA
MGON PO NAS DUS 'KHOR RGYUD 'GREL ZHIB TU GSAN TE BSGOMS PAS
RTOGS PA BRNYES, GZHAN STONG GI LTA BA'I SROL PHYE, YIG CHA 'GA'

GA-YU THOG  GA-YU'I RGYA PHIBS TE GA-YU RTZI CAN GYI THOG
PHIBS,...

GA-YU THOG RNYING MA YON TAN MGON PO, SPYI LO'I DUS RABS BRGYAD
PA'I SA MO SBRUL GYI LOR STOD LUNG SKYID SNA RU YAB GA-YU THOG
KHYUNG PO RDO RJE DANG, YUM RGYA PA CHOS SGRON GNYIS KYI SRAS SU
SPREL ZLA'I TSES BCO LNGA NYIN SKU 'KHRUNGS, DGUNG LO GSUM GYI
THOG RANG GI YAB LAS YI GE 'BRI KLOG DANG, GSO DPYAD KYI GZHUNG
LUGS GSAN PAS TSEGS MED DU MKHYEN TE NAD PA BSKYANGS, DGUNG LO
LNGA PAR YAB LAS BDUD RTZI SMAN SGRUB DANG, SMAN BLA'I SGRUB
THABS RJES GNANG DANG BCAS PA ZHUS, DGUNG LO BCU'I THOG CHOS
RGYAL MES AAG TSOM GYIS SPYAN DRANGS NAS BSAM YAS SU PHEBS,
RGYAL POS NYAMS SAD BLANG PHYIR BRANG TI RGYAL GNYER MKHAR PHUG
SOGS BOD KYI MKHAS PA RNAMS DANG RTZOD DU BCUG PAS KUN LAS RNAM
PAR RGYAL TE BOD SMAN MKHAS PA MI DGU'I GTZO BOR GYUR, RGYA GAR
GYI SMAN PA SHANTI GARBHA DANG, RGYA NAG GI SMAN PA STONG GSUM
GANG BA SOGS YUL PHYOGS GZHAN NAS GDAN DRANGS PA'I BLA SMAN
MKHAS PA MI DGUS DRI BA MI 'DRA BA BTON PAS DE DAG LA SGRA TSAD
RIG PA'I SGO NAS DE DANG MTHUN PA'I LAN BTAB STE, RGYA BOD MKHAS
PA YONGS KYI GTZUG TU BKUR NAS MI YUL DU BYON PA'I SANGS RGYAS
SMAN BLA ZHES GRAGS, CHOS RGYAL MES AAG TSOM DANG, KHRI SRONG
LDE BTZAN GNYIS KYI BLA SMAN PA MDZAD, DGUNG LO NYER LNGA THOG
RGYA GAR DU THENGS DANG PO PHEBS PA DANG RIM BZHIN THENGS GSUM
PHEBS TE PAn CHEN TZANDR'A BH'I DANG, MKHAS PA ME DBANG SOGS
SLOB DPON DU MA BSTEN NAS DPAL LDAN RGYUD BZHI'I KHA SKONG MU
TIG PHRENG BA DANG, THUR DPYAD GNAD KYI LDE MIG SOGS GDAMS NGAG
MANG PO GSAN, RGYA NAG RI BO RTZE LNGAR THENGS GCIG PHEBS TE
'PHAGS PA 'JAM DPAL GYI MDUN NAS SBYOR BA'I PHRENG BA DANG,
BYANG KHOG DON 'GREMS SOGS GDAMS NGAG DU MA ZHUS NAS BOD DU
PHEBS TE GANGS CAN BOD YUL GYI SMAN GYI RIG PAS GZHI BYAS, DE'I
STENG RGYA GAR NAG GYI SLOB DPON RNAMS KYI GDAMS NGAG DANG, BE
RO TZA NAS BSGYUR PA'I PHYOGS GZHAN GYI GSO BA RIG PA'I 'GYUR
DAG GI DGONGS BCUD RNAMS BLANGS NAS KHA SNON MDZAD DE DPAL LDAN
RGYUD BZHI

@2622

ZHES PA'I MA PHYI BSKRUN, BAL PO'I RGYAL PO HA RDA RU GRANG BA
THUR 'BABS KYI NAD BCOS PA SOGS SKU TSE GANG POR GSO RIG BSTAN
DON KHO NA MDZAD, GDUNG RGYUD 'DZIN PA'I SRAS 'BUM SENG DANG,
DPAL 'BUM, DGA' DGA' GSUM 'KHRUNGS, KONG PO BDE RGYAL SOGS SLOB
MA'I TSOGS KYIS BOD YUL GYI SA CHEN PO 'DI GANG BAR BSKRUN,
DGUNG LO BRGYA DANG NYI SHU RTZA LNGA'I THOG 'DAS,...

ZHIG  ...

GA-YU THOG GSAR MA YON TAN MGON PO, GA-YU THOG RNYING MA YON TAN
MGON PO NAS BRTZIS PA'I GDUNG RABS BCU GSUM PA RAB BYUNG GNYIS
PA'I NANG GTZANG NYANG STOD SGO BZHI RE THANG DU 'KHRUNGS, DGUNG
LO BRGYAD KYI STENG GSO RIG LA THUGS GZHOL TE GSAN BSAM MDZAD
PAS MKHAS PAR GYUR, DGUNG LO BCU'I THOG MANG MKHAR TSA LUNG BA
ROG STON DKON MCHOG SKYABS LAS DPAL LDAN RGYUD BZHI RDZOGS PAR
ZHUS, DGUNG LO BCO BRGYAD PA NAS RGYA GAR LA RIM BZHIN THENGS
DRUG PHEBS TE MKHA' 'GRO'I GTZO MO DPAL LDAN PHRENG BA DANG,
DRANG SRONG TZA RA KA SOGS BSTEN NAS GSO DPYAD KYI GZHUNG LUGS
THAMS CAD THUGS SU CHUD PAR GSAN PAS MKHAS PA'I GRAGS PAS PHYOGS
KUN LA KHYAB PAR GYUR, RDO RJE GDAN DU PAn CHEN BRGYA PHRAG DU
MA'I TSOGS DPON MDZAD, SLAR BOD DU PHEBS NAS LUS CAN DU MA NA BA
DANG 'CHI BA LAS SKYOB PAR MDZAD CING, PHYI RABS KYI RJES 'JUG
DANG BU SLOB RNAMS KYI DON DU BRGYAD PA CHE CHUNG GI SNYING PO
BSDUS PA DANG, DPA' BO'I SNYING PO BSDUS PA'I MDO GNAS KYI 'GREL
PA MTHONG BA'I ME LONG SOGS BRTZAMS, KHYAD PAR DU DPAL LDAN
RGYUD BZHI 'DI NYID GSO DPYAD KUN GYI YANG RTZER GZIGS NAS SKAD
GSAR BCAD KYIS GTAN LA PHAB STE GSER MCHAN DANG, ZONG MCHAN
GNYIS BTAB, GZHAN YANG YUL DUS SOGS DGOS KHYAD KYI DBANG GIS
SKABS SU BAB PA'I ZHAL SKONG CI RIGS MDZAD, RGYUD KYI GZHUNG
'GREL MAN NGAG KHA SKONG DANG BCAS PA'I GO CHOD DU CHA LAG BCO
BRGYAD LEGS PAR BSGRIGS NAS SKAL LDAN GYI THUGS SRAS YE SHES
GZUNGS LA GDAMS, RJE 'DI NYID LA RGYUD 'DZIN GYI BU SLOB GRANGS
LAS 'DAS PA BYUNG BA'I GTZO BO NI SUM STON YE SHES GZUNGS KYIS
DBU MDZAD PA'I LJANG SMAN LEB SE DANG, 'BAL SMAN NYI MA, STON PA
AA TSES,
